!!

!

   subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixes_singles_41_p_ccsd(wf, sigma_A_ai, g_IVov, s2_VIvovo)
!!
!! Generated function
!!
      implicit none
!
      class(p_ccsd), intent(in) :: wf
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(inout) :: sigma_A_ai
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_o,wf%n_v), intent(in) :: g_IVov
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(in) :: s2_VIvovo
!
      real(dp), dimension(:,:), allocatable :: X1
!
      call mem%alloc(X1, wf%n_v, wf%n_o)
      call sort_to_21(g_IVov, X1, wf%n_o, wf%n_v)
!
      call dgemv('T', &
         wf%n_v*wf%n_o, &
         wf%n_v*wf%n_o, &
         one, &
         s2_VIvovo, &
         wf%n_v*wf%n_o, &
         X1, 1, &
         one, &
         sigma_A_ai, 1)
!
      call mem%dealloc(X1)
!
   end subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixes_singles_41_p_ccsd

   subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixes_singles_42_p_ccsd(wf, sigma_A_ai, g_IVov, s2_VIvovo)
!!
!! Generated function
!!
      implicit none
!
      class(p_ccsd), intent(in) :: wf
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(inout) :: sigma_A_ai
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_o,wf%n_v), intent(in) :: g_IVov
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(in) :: s2_VIvovo
!
      real(dp), dimension(:,:), allocatable :: X1
      real(dp), dimension(:,:,:,:), allocatable :: X2
!
      call mem%alloc(X1, wf%n_v, wf%n_o)
      call sort_to_21(g_IVov, X1, wf%n_o, wf%n_v)
      call mem%alloc(X2, wf%n_v, wf%n_o, wf%n_v, wf%n_o)
      call sort_to_1432(s2_VIvovo, X2, wf%n_v, wf%n_o, wf%n_v, wf%n_o)
!
      call dgemv('T', &
         wf%n_v*wf%n_o, &
         wf%n_v*wf%n_o, &
         -half, &
         X2, &
         wf%n_v*wf%n_o, &
         X1, 1, &
         one, &
         sigma_A_ai, 1)
!
      call mem%dealloc(X1)
      call mem%dealloc(X2)
!
   end subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixes_singles_42_p_ccsd

   subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixes_singles_43_p_ccsd(wf, sigma_A_ai, C1_V, g_IVoo, s_VIvo)
!!
!! Generated function
!!
      implicit none
!
      class(p_ccsd), intent(in) :: wf
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%positronic_active_space,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(inout) :: sigma_A_ai
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%positronic_active_space), intent(in) :: C1_V
      real(dp), dimension(wf%positronic_active_space,wf%n_o,wf%n_o), intent(in) :: g_IVoo
      real(dp), dimension(wf%positronic_active_space,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(in) :: s_VIvo
!
      real(dp), dimension(:), allocatable :: X1
      real(dp), dimension(:,:), allocatable :: X2
!
      integer :: i1, i2
!
      call mem%alloc(X1, wf%positronic_active_space)
      call zero_array(X1, wf%positronic_active_space)
!
      do i2 = 1, wf%n_o
         do i1 = 1, wf%positronic_active_space
            X1(i1) = X1(i1) + g_IVoo(i1,i2,i2)
         end do
      end do
!
      call mem%alloc(X2, wf%n_v, wf%n_o)
!
      call dgemv('T', &
         wf%positronic_active_space, &
         wf%n_v*wf%n_o, &
         one, &
         s_VIvo, &
         wf%positronic_active_space, &
         X1, 1, &
         zero, &
         X2, 1)
!
      call mem%dealloc(X1)
!
      call dger(wf%positronic_active_space, &
         wf%n_v*wf%n_o, &
         one, &
         C1_V, 1, &
         X2, 1, &
         sigma_A_ai, &
         wf%positronic_active_space)
!
      call mem%dealloc(X2)
!
   end subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixes_singles_43_p_ccsd

   subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixes_singles_48_p_ccsd(wf, sigma_A_ai, C1_V, g_IVoo, s_AIvo)
!!
!! Generated function
!!
      implicit none
!
      class(p_ccsd), intent(in) :: wf
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(inout) :: sigma_A_ai
!
      real(dp), intent(in) :: C1_V, s_AIvo
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_o,wf%n_o), intent(in) :: g_IVoo
!
      real(dp) :: X1
!
      integer :: i1
!
      X1 = zero
!
      do i1 = 1, wf%n_o
         X1 = X1 + g_IVoo(i1,i1)
      end do
!
      sigma_A_ai = sigma_A_ai + C1_V*s_AIvo * X1
!
   end subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixes_singles_48_p_ccsd

   subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixes_singles_49_p_ccsd(wf, sigma_A_ai, C1_V, h_IV, s_AIvo)

   end subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixes_singles_49_p_ccsd

   subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixes_singles_49_p_ccsd(wf, sigma_A_ai, C1_V_vo, g_AVoo)
!!
!! Generated function
!!
      implicit none
!
      class(p_ccsd), intent(in) :: wf
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%positronic_active_space,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(inout) :: sigma_A_ai
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%positronic_active_space,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(in) :: C1_V_vo
      real(dp), dimension(wf%positronic_active_space,wf%positronic_active_space,wf%n_o,wf%n_o), intent(in) :: g_AVoo
!
      real(dp), dimension(:,:), allocatable :: X1
!
      integer :: i1, i2, i3
!
      call mem%alloc(X1, wf%positronic_active_space, wf%positronic_active_space)
      call zero_array(X1, wf%positronic_active_space**2)
!
      do i3 = 1, wf%n_o
         do i2 = 1, wf%positronic_active_space
            do i1 = 1, wf%positronic_active_space
               X1(i1,i2) = X1(i1,i2) + g_AVoo(i1,i2,i3,i3)
            end do
         end do
      end do
!
!
      call dgemm('N', 'N', &
         wf%positronic_active_space, &
         wf%n_v*wf%n_o, &
         wf%positronic_active_space, &
         -half, &
         X1, &
         wf%positronic_active_space, &
         C1_V_vo, &
         wf%positronic_active_space, &
         one, &
         sigma_A_ai, &
         wf%positronic_active_space)
!
      call mem%dealloc(X1)
!
   end subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixes_singles_49_p_ccsd

   subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixes_singles_24_p_ccsd(wf, sigma_A_ai, C1_V_vo, S_AIai, g_AVoo)
!!
!! Generated function
!!
      implicit none
!
      class(p_ccsd), intent(in) :: wf
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(inout) :: sigma_A_ai
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_o,wf%n_v), intent(in) :: g_AVoo
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(in) :: C1_V_vo, S_AIai
!
      real(dp) :: X2
      real(dp), dimension(:,:), allocatable :: X1
!
      real(dp), external :: ddot
!
      call mem%alloc(X1, wf%n_v, wf%n_o)
      call sort_to_21(g_AVoo, X1, wf%n_o, wf%n_v)
      X2 = half * ddot(wf%n_v*wf%n_o, X1, 1, S_AIai, 1)
      call mem%dealloc(X1)
      call daxpy(wf%n_v*wf%n_o, X2, C1_V_vo, 1, sigma_A_ai, 1)
!
   end subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixes_singles_24_p_ccsd

      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_o,wf%n_o,wf%n_v,wf%n_v), intent(in) :: g_oovv
!
      real(dp), dimension(:,:,:,:), allocatable :: X1
!
      call mem%alloc(X1, wf%n_o, wf%n_o, wf%n_v, wf%n_o)
!
      call dgemm('N', 'N', &
         wf%n_v*wf%n_o**2, &
         wf%n_o, &
         wf%n_v, &
         -half, &
         g_oovv, &
         wf%n_v*wf%n_o**2, &
         S_AIaibj, &
         wf%n_v, &
         zero, &
         X1, &
         wf%n_v*wf%n_o**2)
!
!
      call dgemm('N', 'N', &
         wf%n_v, &
         wf%n_v*wf%n_o**2, &
         wf%n_o, &
         one, &
         c0_vo, &
         wf%n_v, &
         X1, &
         wf%n_o, &
         one, &
         rho_A_aibj, &
         wf%n_v)
!
      call mem%dealloc(X1)
!
   end subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixed_doubles_20_p_ccsd

   subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixed_doubles_25_p_ccsd(wf, rho_A_aibj, S_AIaibj, c0_vo, g_IIov)
!!
!! Generated function
!!
      implicit none
!
      class(p_ccsd), intent(in) :: wf
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(inout) :: rho_A_aibj
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_o,wf%n_v), intent(in) :: g_IIov
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(in) :: c0_vo
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(in) :: S_AIaibj
!
      real(dp) :: X2
      real(dp), dimension(:,:), allocatable :: X1
!
      real(dp), external :: ddot
!
      call mem%alloc(X1, wf%n_o, wf%n_v)
      call sort_to_21(c0_vo, X1, wf%n_v, wf%n_o)
      X2 = half * ddot(wf%n_v*wf%n_o, X1, 1, g_IIov, 1)
      call mem%dealloc(X1)
      call add_3412_to_1234(X2, S_AIaibj, rho_A_aibj, wf%n_v, wf%n_o, wf%n_v, wf%n_o)
!
   end subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixed_doubles_25_p_ccsd

   subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixed_doubles_26_p_ccsd(wf, rho_A_aibj, c0_vo, g_AIov, t_vovo)

   subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixed_doubles_50_p_ccsd(wf, rho_A_aibj, S_AIaibj, c0_vo, g_AVov)
!!
!! Generated function
!!
      implicit none
!
      class(p_ccsd), intent(in) :: wf
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(inout) :: rho_A_aibj
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_o,wf%n_v), intent(in) :: g_AVov
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(in) :: c0_vo
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(in) :: S_AIaibj
!
      real(dp) :: X2
      real(dp), dimension(:,:), allocatable :: X1
!
      real(dp), external :: ddot
!
      call mem%alloc(X1, wf%n_o, wf%n_v)
      call sort_to_21(c0_vo, X1, wf%n_v, wf%n_o)
      X2 =  -ddot(wf%n_v*wf%n_o, X1, 1, g_AVov, 1)
      call mem%dealloc(X1)
      call add_3412_to_1234(X2, S_AIaibj, rho_A_aibj, wf%n_v, wf%n_o, wf%n_v, wf%n_o)
!
   end subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixed_doubles_50_p_ccsd

   subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixed_doubles_55_p_ccsd(wf, rho_A_aibj, S_AIvo, S_BIvo, c0_vo, g_IVov)
!!
!! Generated function
!!
      implicit none
!
      class(p_ccsd), intent(in) :: wf
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(inout) :: rho_A_aibj
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_o,wf%n_v), intent(in) :: g_IVov
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(in) :: S_AIvo, S_BIvo, c0_vo
!
      real(dp) :: X2
      real(dp), dimension(:,:), allocatable :: X1
!
      real(dp), external :: ddot
!
      call mem%alloc(X1, wf%n_o, wf%n_v)
      call sort_to_21(c0_vo, X1, wf%n_v, wf%n_o)
      X2 = ddot(wf%n_v*wf%n_o, X1, 1, g_IVov, 1)
      call mem%dealloc(X1)
!
      call dger(wf%n_v*wf%n_o, &
         wf%n_v*wf%n_o, &
         X2, &
         S_BIvo, 1, &
         S_AIvo, 1, &
         rho_A_aibj, &
         wf%n_v*wf%n_o)
!
!
   end subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixed_doubles_55_p_ccsd

!!
!! Generated function
!!
      implicit none
!
      class(p_ccsd), intent(in) :: wf
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(inout) :: rho_A_aibj

!
      real(dp), dimension(:,:), allocatable :: X1, X2, X3
      real(dp), dimension(:,:,:,:), allocatable :: X4
!
      call mem%alloc(X1, wf%n_o, wf%n_v)
      call sort_to_21(c0_vo, X1, wf%n_v, wf%n_o)
      call mem%alloc(X2, wf%n_o, wf%n_v)

         wf%n_v*wf%n_o, &

         -half, &

         X1, 1, &
         zero, &
         X2, 1)

      call mem%alloc(X3, wf%n_o, wf%n_o)

         X2, &

         S_AIvo, &
         wf%n_v, &
         zero, &

      call mem%alloc(X4, wf%n_v, wf%n_o, wf%n_v, wf%n_o)
      call sort_to_3412(t_vovo, X4, wf%n_v, wf%n_o, wf%n_v, wf%n_o)
!
      call dgemm('N', 'N', &
         wf%n_v**2*wf%n_o, &

         wf%n_v**2*wf%n_o, &

      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(in) :: c2_vovo
!
      real(dp), dimension(:,:), allocatable :: X1
!
      call mem%alloc(X1, wf%n_v, wf%n_v)
!
      call dgemm('T', 'T', &
         wf%n_v, &
         wf%n_v, &
         wf%n_o, &
         one, &
         g_AVov, &
         wf%n_o, &
         s_VIvo, &
         wf%n_v, &
         zero, &
         X1, &
         wf%n_v)
!
!
      call dgemm('T', 'N', &
         wf%n_v, &
         wf%n_v*wf%n_o**2, &
         wf%n_v, &
         one, &
         X1, &
         wf%n_v, &
         c2_vovo, &
         wf%n_v, &
         one, &
         rho_A_aibj, &
         wf%n_v)
!
      call mem%dealloc(X1)
!
   end subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixed_doubles_121_p_ccsd

   subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixed_doubles_122_p_ccsd(wf, rho_A_aibj, c2_vovo, g_AVov, s_VIvo)
!!
!! Generated function
!!
      implicit none
!
      class(p_ccsd), intent(in) :: wf
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(inout) :: rho_A_aibj

      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(in) :: s_VIvo

      call sort_to_21(g_AVov, X1, wf%n_o, wf%n_v)
      call mem%alloc(X2, wf%n_v, wf%n_o, wf%n_v, wf%n_o)

         X3, 1)

      call mem%dealloc(X2)

         s_VIvo, 1, &
         rho_A_aibj, &

   subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixed_doubles_151_p_ccsd(wf, rho_A_aibj, g_IIoo, p3_AI, t_vovo)
!!
!! Generated function
!!
      implicit none
!
      class(p_ccsd), intent(in) :: wf
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(inout) :: rho_A_aibj
!
      real(dp), intent(in) :: p3_AI
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_o,wf%n_o), intent(in) :: g_IIoo
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(in) :: t_vovo
!
      real(dp), dimension(:,:,:,:), allocatable :: X1
!
      call mem%alloc(X1, wf%n_v, wf%n_o, wf%n_v, wf%n_o)
      call sort_to_3412(t_vovo, X1, wf%n_v, wf%n_o, wf%n_v, wf%n_o)
!
      call dgemm('N', 'N', &
         wf%n_v**2*wf%n_o, &
         wf%n_o, &
         wf%n_o, &
         -0.5*p3_AI, &
         X1, &
         wf%n_v**2*wf%n_o, &
         g_IIoo, &
         wf%n_o, &
         one, &
         rho_A_aibj, &
         wf%n_v**2*wf%n_o)
!
      call mem%dealloc(X1)
!
   end subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixed_doubles_151_p_ccsd

!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(inout) :: rho_A_aibj
!
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_o,wf%n_v), intent(in) :: F_ov
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(in) :: p_AIvo
      real(dp), dimension(wf%n_v,wf%n_o,wf%n_v,wf%n_o), intent(in) :: t_vovo
!
      real(dp), dimension(:,:), allocatable :: X1
      real(dp), dimension(:,:,:,:), allocatable :: X2
!
      call mem%alloc(X1, wf%n_v, wf%n_v)
!
      call dgemm('T', 'T', &
         wf%n_v, &
         wf%n_v, &
         wf%n_o, &
         -0.500000000000000, &
         F_ov, &
         wf%n_o, &
         p_AIvo, &
         wf%n_v, &
         zero, &
         X1, &
         wf%n_v)
!
      call mem%alloc(X2, wf%n_v, wf%n_o, wf%n_v, wf%n_o)
!
      call dgemm('T', 'N', &
         wf%n_v, &
         wf%n_v*wf%n_o**2, &
         wf%n_v, &
         one, &
         X1, &
         wf%n_v, &
         t_vovo, &
         wf%n_v, &
         zero, &
         X2, &
         wf%n_v)
!
      call mem%dealloc(X1)
      call add_3412_to_1234(one, X2, rho_A_aibj, wf%n_v, wf%n_o, wf%n_v, wf%n_o)
      call mem%dealloc(X2)

   end subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixed_doubles_189_p_ccsd

         wf%n_v*wf%n_o, &
         wf%n_v*wf%n_o, &
         -0.500000000000000, &
         u_vovo, &
         wf%n_v*wf%n_o, &
         X1, 1, &
         zero, &
         X2, 1)
!
      call mem%dealloc(X1)
!

         wf%n_v*wf%n_o, &
         one, &
         p_VIvo, 1, &
         X2, 1, &
         rho_A_aibj, &
         wf%n_v*wf%n_o)
!
      call mem%dealloc(X2)
!
   end subroutine jacobian_p_ccsd_mixed_doubles_235_p_ccsd

!!
!! Generated function
!!
      implicit none
!
      class(p_ccsd), intent(in) :: wf
